import requests

headers = {
    'accept': 'application/json',
    'accept-language': 'en-GB,en-US;q=0.9,en;q=0.8',
    'content-type': 'application/json',
    'if-none-match': 'W/"12103-DhFfKuHAX8smFMGYIcqoG1HVhXk"',
    'origin': 'https://sarmaaya.pk',
    'priority': 'u=1, i',
    'sec-ch-ua': '"Not;A=Brand";v="8", "Chromium";v="150", "Google Chrome";v="150"',
    'sec-ch-ua-mobile': '?0',
    'sec-ch-ua-platform': '"Windows"',
    'sec-fetch-dest': 'empty',
    'sec-fetch-mode': 'cors',
    'sec-fetch-site': 'same-site',
    'user-agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/150.0.0.0 Safari/537.36',
}

params = {
    'page': '1',
    'limit': '100',
}

response = requests.get('https://beta-restapi.sarmaaya.pk/api/indices/KMIALLSHR/companies', params=params, headers=headers)

print(response.status_code)
print(response.text)

KMIALLSHR API

import requests

headers = {
    'accept': 'application/json',
    'accept-language': 'en-GB,en-US;q=0.9,en;q=0.8',
    'content-type': 'application/json',
    'if-none-match': 'W/"a0ca-qNmHKz4VT44lybxmAX8mRA+0e+A"',
    'origin': 'https://sarmaaya.pk',
    'priority': 'u=1, i',
    'sec-ch-ua': '"Not;A=Brand";v="8", "Chromium";v="150", "Google Chrome";v="150"',
    'sec-ch-ua-mobile': '?0',
    'sec-ch-ua-platform': '"Windows"',
    'sec-fetch-dest': 'empty',
    'sec-fetch-mode': 'cors',
    'sec-fetch-site': 'same-site',
    'user-agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/150.0.0.0 Safari/537.36',
}

response = requests.get('https://beta-restapi.sarmaaya.pk/api/indices/sunbrust/KMIALLSHR', headers=headers)

print(response.status_code)
print(response.text)

}
